## La Medusa was scheduled for the match. Halcon 814 says she was announced hospitalized halfway through the show and needed an emergency appendix surgery. Rossy Moreno did well as an emergency sub but lost when a plancha missed Irma and hit the referee Gran Davis by mistake. Fans thought Moreno was the better wrestler.
5) Cien Caras COR Siglo XX [mask]
## Siglo XX is José Luis Pérez Rodríguez. He quickly end up under a new mask as Killer. Bloody, dramatic match. Match ends in a countout when Siglo missed on a pescado, Cien beats him up a little, and comes back in for the countout. Halcon says Siglo was also taken to the hospital.
